Such driving capital out of the industry not only makes the national economy increasingly depleted, but also drives fish into the abyss, helping the international economic invasion. This is the sixth. Seventh, inertia and hesitation, following emotions and not being able to bear resentment. As mentioned above, the politics of today are full of flaws and evils, and the measures taken are also inappropriate. However, I have not heard of a special agency specially investigating and prosecuting a person who abuses the law for personal gain, nor have I heard of a chief official in charge punishing a person who exceeds the law and disrupts the discipline. They are mostly constrained by emotions, observing the situation, knowing what they mean but afraid to act. They have become accustomed to it and are afraid to be the first. They tolerate each other and forgive each other, only forgetting the responsibilities assigned by the party and the country, and selling favors. There has never been a person who stands up to break all restrictions and bear the responsibility of rectifying discipline for the country. How can we seek to clarify politics in this way? Therefore, the lack of vigor in today's laws and disciplines is not only due to the lack of implementation of the supervisory system, but also because the atmosphere of hating evil as if it were an enemy is disappearing day by day. This is the seventh.

(3) Reasons for Establishing a Policy Center and Policy Guidelines in the Shortest Possible Time: The improvement of the system and the rectification of discipline are as described above. If we want to improve administrative efficiency and make the people benefit from politics, we must weigh the importance and urgency, and determine a concise and practical plan to select one or two of the most urgent cases and concentrate all efforts to achieve them. As the ancient saying goes, knowing what to do first is the great principle of governing. The most harsh criticism of our party's politics is "everything

Page 8

is done, but nothing is accomplished." Although this is the criticism of the streets, it is enough for our self-reflection. After a major change in the country, the national strength and the people's strength are both exhausted. Those who are in charge of administration, if they do not understand the limitations of the facts and only have the mentality of seeking quick success, make plans that are detailed and comprehensive. No matter how beautiful the plan is, it will inevitably fall into the predicament of being unable to advance or retreat due to the country's financial resources. As a result, agencies are established everywhere, businesses are suspended, and talents and national resources are not economical. Moreover, today, when the military is roughly settled and the bandits and communists are rampant, it is especially appropriate to prioritize what should be prioritized and postpone what should be postponed. Therefore, the central government should determine the policy center of the country and the policy guidelines of the local government within the shortest period of one year, and devote the spiritual and material strength of the whole country to ensure that it is implemented. On the negative side, we should remove the worst and most harmful things, focus all our efforts on removing the most harmful and most criticized things to the nation. On the positive side, we should also concentrate our efforts on rectifying the most important and urgent prerequisites for the stability and progress of all government affairs. Local administration should also determine its most important work guidelines under the two major conditions of stabilizing the people's livelihood and cultivating the people's strength, so that they are consistent with the central government's policy center and do not conflict with each other. Once the goals are simple and the strength is concentrated, then the general principles will be clear and the specific details will be clear. If it is implemented for a year, it will be effective. Based on the above reasons, I respectfully propose the following items:

A. Regarding the Reform of the Central System and Organization (A) Enforce that over two-thirds of the members of the Central Political Council permanently reside in the Central Government. (B) Strengthen the organization of the Secretariat of the Central Political Council; All special secretaries of various groups such as diplomacy, military affairs, finance, economics, education, law, and local autonomy must be fully established. (C) The political vice ministers of the various departments of the Executive Yuan shall be filled by the special secretaries of the related groups of the Political Council, and all official documents of the various departments, whether internal or external, must be countersigned by the political vice minister in order to be valid. (D) Revise the regulations concerning the State Council and the Executive Yuan Council in the Organic Law of the National Government. (E) The organization of the Executive Yuan should be changed as follows: (1) The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce should be merged into the Ministry of Industry. (2) The Ministry of Health should be merged into the Ministry of Interior. (3) The Construction Commission should focus on designing and guiding national construction and should not be listed as an administrative agency and should be directly under the National Government. The model projects that have been tried should continue to be implemented, but no new projects should be created, so as to design well and focus on urging the development of private enterprises. (4) The organization of other ministries and commissions should be reduced as much as possible, and the number of personnel should be strictly determined and decided by the Central Political Council.

B. Regarding the Program for Rectifying Discipline and Refreshing Politics (A) The National Government shall issue a general amnesty on New Year's Day of the Republic of China in 1920, except for the heinous criminals who betrayed the Party and the country and the communists, other political prisoners should be pardoned to show leniency. The Judicial Yuan shall discuss the scope, hand it over to the Legislative Yuan for discussion, and submit it to the National Government for execution. (B) The Central Government shall order the National Government to earnestly admonish all agencies that they must not have the bad habits of procrastination, sloth, fragmentation, and division. Each agency must be vigorous and responsible. (C) The Supervisory Yuan shall be established within a time limit to implement the supervisory powers, and the regulations on the punishment of supervisory personnel for dereliction of duty and misconduct shall be formulated. (D) The powers and responsibilities of the various ministries and commissions shall be clearly defined. For matters involving more than one department, the department responsible for the main business shall be determined according to its nature and decided by the Central Political Council. The scope of powers and responsibilities shall be clearly defined, especially regarding the management and operation of state-owned enterprises, so that private enterprises can be guaranteed. (E) Various laws and regulations for implementing examinations at all levels and implementing qualifications and selections shall be implemented within a time limit, and each agency shall be required to send a detailed table of personnel advances and retreats and the number of personnel and salaries every three months to the superior agency. If the qualification of the personnel is concealed or the personnel is employed beyond the quota, the chief official in charge shall be punished. (F) Implement the reduction of government, cut and merge redundant agencies, and abolish them. The Central Political Council shall decide on the principles and hand them over to the National Government for implementation at each level. (G) The Accounting Office shall be established within a time limit and be directly under the National Government. All central agencies shall be limited to the end of December this year, and local governments shall be limited to March of 1920, to prepare the agency budget for the fiscal year and the budget within its scope of responsibility, and submit it to the National Government for approval. Thereafter, the revenue and expenditure statements and supporting documents of each agency must be sent in accordance with the law for review and approval. Those who violate the law shall be admonished or punished, and the chief official in charge shall be punished. If the audit finds expenditures that do not comply with legal procedures or evidence of fraud, the audit agency shall submit it to the Supervisory Yuan for handling. (H) The Legislative Yuan shall formulate regulations for punishing corruption and embezzlement. If an official receives bribes or embezzles public funds, and the amount is more than a certain amount, the National Government shall impose life imprisonment or the death penalty in accordance with the extraordinary procedure and confiscate his property. (I) Strict regulations on the leave of political officials shall be formulated to restrict officials from taking leave and leaving their jobs at will, and to stipulate the punishment for absenteeism. It is absolutely forbidden for officials to hold positions in commercial institutions or to engage in speculative market transactions, and it is stipulated that central political officials shall not hold local administrative positions. (J) According to the central government's resolution, the Accounting Bureau shall be established within a time limit to implement the unification of accounting. Hereafter, the various ministries and commissions shall no longer be allowed to directly allocate the funds within their scope of responsibility in the name of special accounting. All national income and Geng funds, regardless of their nature, must be deposited in the Central Bank and the National Bank acting as the national treasury, and the establishment of various banks by the various ministries and commissions is strictly prohibited in order to achieve the effect of unification.

C. Policy Center and Policy Guidelines within the Shortest Possible Time (A) The goal of politics within the next year should be to stabilize order and cultivate the people's strength, concentrate efforts to eliminate the greatest evils, and meet the country's most urgent needs. (B) The policy center of the Central Government: (1) On the negative side, focus on the work of eliminating communism, suppressing bandits, banning opium, and abolishing likin. (2) On the positive side, focus on military rehabilitation and financial consolidation. Secondly, if there is any spare energy, then develop transportation and water conservancy. (C) The policy guidelines of the local government should focus on (1) eliminating bandits, (2) investigating household registration, (3) establishing Baojia system, (4) encouraging agricultural production, (5) popularizing education, and rectifying the academic atmosphere, and finally on the promotion of local autonomy and the completion of the autonomous organization. (D) Regarding the elimination of communism and the suppression of bandits, the central government should regard it as the most important and urgent task, and the party, government, army, and people should cooperate with all their strength and earnestly cooperate, and strive to complete it within three to six months. In necessary areas, temporary overall command organs may be established, and the measures shall be decided by the Central Political Council. (E) Starting from January 1 of 1920, a three-year limit shall be set for completing the opium ban. One-third shall be reduced each year, and the ban shall be completely eliminated by the end of the third year. The Special Tax Agency and the Opium Prohibition Committee shall jointly handle it. After the central government promulgates the measures, if anyone privately transports drugs and is found, the National Government may impose additional punishments in accordance with extraordinary procedures. (F) It is decided to implement the abolition of likin on January 1 of 1920, and the provinces shall not request an extension for any reason. (G) Commend those who have worked hard for the revolution and have made contributions to the country and society, and the state shall grant them annuities. (H) The following are the guidelines for military rehabilitation: (1) Military rehabilitation includes the following tasks, which shall be completed within six months to one year: 1. Determination of the establishment and enrichment of the troop strength, 2. Clearance of arrears of pay, 3. Elimination and resettlement of the old and weak, 4. Placement and accommodation of officers and soldiers outside the quota, 5. Rehabilitation of wounded and sick soldiers, and compensation for deceased officers and soldiers, 6. Formulation of preliminary national defense plans, 7. Regulations on the military regions other than the bandit suppression troops, 8. Closure of wartime agencies and clearance of the anti-rebel military expenses, 9. Reorganization and replenishment of clothing and military supplies. (2) The expenses for military rehabilitation shall be raised separately and shall not hinder the budget for normal government and military expenses. However, the construction of other positive aspects within this one-year period should be appropriately reduced or postponed. No department shall issue public bonds for matters under its jurisdiction, and those that have been issued but have not been fully raised shall be postponed. (3) The special funds raised for military rehabilitation shall be managed by the Central Military and Political Organs together with the financial industry and related groups to organize a Special Fund Management Committee for Military Rehabilitation. All revenue and expenditure shall be reported publicly. (I) Regarding local autonomy, it shall be urged to proceed in accordance with the original procedures, and attention shall be paid to the organization and selection of personnel in the district, township, and town offices, so that the outstanding elements of the local middle-level society and the honest and reliable people of the countryside can live peacefully in their hometown, follow the doctrine of our party, and participate in the work of local autonomy as much as possible. The measures shall be formulated by the Central Training Department and the Ministry of Interior. (J) Regarding the consolidation of finance, the clearance of internal and external debts, and the establishment of a financial foundation, the Ministry of Finance shall formulate a plan within a time limit and submit it for approval.

As mentioned above, without improving the central system and organization, there is no way to expect the agile implementation of government affairs. Without vigorously rectifying discipline, there is no way to improve administrative efficiency. In particular, without establishing a political work center in the shortest possible time, there is no way to concentrate efforts and achieve practical results. Therefore, based on what I have seen, I propose the above. Whether it is appropriate or not, please decide."

Proposal to Eliminate Communist Bandits within a Time Limit

Wang Zhengting proposed a proposal to eliminate communist bandits in various places within a time limit. The original text said: Since the Yan-Feng rebellion, communist bandits in various places have taken the opportunity to be rampant, burning, killing, looting, and raping, which is unbearable to hear. Among them, the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Shaanxi have suffered the most. Now that the rebellion has been quelled, the most important government policy is construction. However, if the communist bandits in various places are not eliminated for one day, then no matter whether it is agriculture, industry, or commerce, people cannot live and work in peace. Even if there is a good plan, it cannot be implemented. Moreover, the methods adopted by the communist bandits are the most cruel. They not only inflict cruelty on the people of our country, but also capture and loot foreigners in various places. Their intention is nothing more than to provoke diplomacy in order to achieve the purpose of destruction. In recent months, looking around the areas with bandits, transportation is blocked, people's livelihood is deteriorating, and all kinds of businesses have gone bankrupt. Under these circumstances, even if the government has a very precise construction plan, I am afraid that it will be a case of drawing a cake to satisfy hunger. I hereby propose that the government mobilize capable troops and strive to eliminate the communist bandits in the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Henan and other places within three months in order to secure the people's livelihood and benefit construction. Whether it is appropriate or not, please decide.

Proposal Regarding Matters Under the Jurisdiction of Construction

Sun Ke proposed that for new construction projects, the government departments in charge should be directly responsible for handling them, and it is not appropriate to establish separate agencies at any time to avoid redundancy and save public funds. The original text reads: "In my humble opinion, the government establishes various departments to manage various undertakings throughout the country. In terms of their duties, they are not only administrative and supervisory bodies, but also responsible for planning and operating various construction projects under their jurisdiction. Moreover, according to the organizational law, each department establishes official positions and employs talented individuals. If the work within the departments is not substantial and the staff are idle, it would be a great loss to the original intention of the government in establishing these departments. However, recently, when the government plans various new construction projects, it often establishes a separate and independent agency for each new project, either because the scale is considered too large, or the progress is too urgent, or even due to personal considerations. Although there may be various reasons for the central government's decision at the time, the resulting malpractices are that various departments cannot interfere with the undertakings under their jurisdiction, lose their duties, and become idle. At the same time, the newly established agencies are large in scale, with numerous staff, and consume tens of thousands of public funds each month. Both talent and finances are uneconomical, and conflicts of authority often occur, which is not a good plan. Now that the great calamity has been quelled and military affairs have ended, the number of new undertakings to be launched will inevitably increase day by day. I believe that all construction projects that should be planned in the future should be handled directly by the relevant departments in charge, in accordance with the provisions of the organizational law of the various departments promulgated by the government, so that redundant agencies will not be established too often, the administrative system will not be disrupted, and the annual savings of public funds will also be considerable. Whether this is appropriate, I respectfully await your public decision."

Proposal on Strictly Prohibiting the Enlistment of Bandits

Liu Zhi proposed strictly prohibiting military division and brigade commanders from enlisting bandits and promoting party-based education to awaken those who have mistakenly joined the Communist Party. The general idea is that since the rise of the revolutionary army, wars have frequently occurred throughout the country, with almost no peaceful year, leading to widespread suffering and mountains full of bandits. During the warlord era, the enlistment of bandits was used to expand personal power, resulting in a cycle of soldiers and bandits, with the quality of soldiers deteriorating and the banditry becoming more rampant. The Communist Party took advantage of this, and the situation became increasingly uncontrollable. Fortunately, the military campaign to suppress the rebellion is about to end, and both Heaven and people desire unification. It is proposed that the conference instruct the National Government to issue an order to all military commanders, prohibiting the enlistment of bandits to curb the source of chaos. As for the Communist Party's thugs who specialize in murder and arson, they should be promptly suppressed by force to prevent them from becoming a prairie fire. A portion of young people, due to their unstable minds, are lured by the Communist Party's heresies and mistakenly embark on the wrong path. Party-based education should be promoted, the essence of the Three People's Principles should be elucidated, and the propaganda power of our party should be expanded, penetrating the inner layers of the people to win their hearts, so that these young people can be awakened, thereby reducing national losses and achieving long-term stability.

Four Proposals for Rectifying Party Affairs

He Chengjun has four proposals on party affairs. The main points are extracted below: (A) Proposal on stipulating the work of party members. The training of party members is one of the most important tasks of our party. The recognition of party doctrine, the observance of party regulations, the cultivation of party morality, and the implementation of resolutions by all party members must be carefully examined and perfected in order to engage in training, and it must be universal and correct in order to be effective. At present, the party departments in various districts are becoming increasingly decadent, and the training work is simply at a standstill. The malpractices have almost led to party members breaking away from the party departments. Those who run the party should earnestly rectify this phenomenon. Party members should also intensify their training. From now on, the provincial party departments should instruct the training departments of the city, county, and district party departments to stipulate the monthly and quarterly work methods for formal and probationary party members, which can be divided into two aspects. First, the scope of work for each formal party member each quarter should be based on the central government's predetermined principles for party member training. The scope of work each month should be determined according to the environment. The completion of the work must be reported in writing, and the party department will use it as a basis for continuous assessment to determine the quality of the performance. Second, the scope of work for probationary party members is the same as above, but during the probationary period, they must cultivate the idea of ​​loyalty to the doctrine and enhance their revolutionary enthusiasm. If their performance is excellent, the directly subordinate party department may submit it to the higher-level party department for approval to be promoted to formal party members. (B) Proposal to reduce the number of county party department units. The general idea is that most of the party departments below the county level cannot connect with the higher-level party departments. To remedy this, the only way is to reduce the number of county party department units in order to engage in the rectification of discipline. The methods are: 1. County divisions with a small number of party members who are ignorant of the people's wisdom will not temporarily establish county party departments. The established district party departments and sub-district party departments will be affiliated to the county party departments and district party departments of their neighboring counties. 2. Those with fewer than 500 party members or fewer than three district party departments will not temporarily establish county party departments, but they may establish directly subordinate district party departments. 3. County divisions that are connected enough to form three or more directly subordinate district party departments may jointly form a county party department. (C) Proposal to train cadres and talents for party departments. Our party is a revolutionary political party, and the Three People's Principles are the guide for our party's efforts. All personnel in charge of party department work must have their personality established and their morality cultivated. They must have a firm understanding of the party's doctrine and hold it permanently, with life and death as their goal and unswerving. Only then can they shoulder the revolutionary task and complete the revolutionary mission. However, a look at the current staff of party departments at all levels is not only insufficient to meet this expectation, but also disappointing. In order to remedy this situation, the most important thing is the training of cadres and talents for party departments. The method should be to establish a party affairs cadre school by the Central Training Department, and implement both examination and selection methods when collecting students. Only in this way can revolutionary talents be selected and practical training results be achieved. As for future service in various places, two points should be noted: 1. The central government must stipulate its work standards and phased plans, and conduct assessments at any time. 2. The treatment should be improved and the living expenses should be increased so as to restrain their greed and cultivate their integrity. (D) Proposal that party affairs inspectors should be concurrently held by Central Committee members and Provincial Committee members. The methods are roughly as follows: (1) During the adjournment of the plenary session of the Central Executive Committee, in addition to the Standing Committee members, the remaining executive and supervisory committee members may concurrently serve as party affairs inspectors and go to various provinces for inspection. (2) The provincial party departments in various provinces, in addition to retaining one of the standing committee members to perform daily affairs, the remaining executive and supervisory committee members may concurrently serve as party affairs inspectors and go to various counties, cities, and districts for inspection. (3) If the central inspector discovers the decadence of party affairs, the errors of work, and the negligence of the provincial committee of the party department of each province during the inspection period, he may submit it to the Central Standing Committee at any time for rectification or punishment. (4) If the provincial inspector discovers the decadence of party affairs, the errors of work, and the negligence of the committee members at all levels of the city, county, and district party departments during the inspection period, he may submit it to the Provincial Standing Committee at any time for rectification or punishment. (5) The central inspectors must submit the entire report to the Central Standing Committee after the inspection results in various provinces, and the Central Standing Committee will then submit it to the plenary session of the Central Executive Committee, so that the direction of promoting party affairs across the country can be determined. (6) The provincial inspectors must submit the entire report to the Standing Committee after the inspection results in various cities, counties, and districts, so that they can clearly understand the actual situation of the lower-level party departments and plan and develop strategies at any time.

Proposal on Conducting Local Self-Government

Chen Zhaoying proposed that in conducting local self-government, we should first pay attention to training personnel, and take into account economic talents, and proceed in an orderly manner. The methods are: (1) In conducting local self-government in each province, the leading county in the old prefectural jurisdiction should be the first to conduct it, and the county magistrates of other counties in the same prefectural jurisdiction should select a number of people who have considerable faith in the local area and gather them in the leading county for training together. (2) The training personnel should be filled by members of the provincial government who do not serve as heads of departments, and other personnel with higher positions and more idle duties, who will go to the leading county for on-site training. (3) The training period shall be set at three months. (4) During the training period, the trainees selected by the counties must be attached to the leading county to conduct local self-government as on-site practice. (5) After the training period expires, the trainees selected by the counties will be sent back to their original counties, and the county magistrate will select those with better performance and report them to the provincial government to be appointed as district chiefs to conduct local self-government in the county.

Proposal on Guaranteeing People's Freedom

Chen Mingshu's proposal to guarantee people's freedom is as follows: "The freedoms of people's person, property, speech, publication, assembly, and association were originally listed in our party's political program, and have also been demonstrated in the declarations and orders issued by the National Government since its establishment. However, during the military administration period, the government had to impose considerable restrictions on various freedoms of the people in order to eliminate obstacles to the revolution. During the political tutelage period, it was also due to the military actions of suppressing the rebellion. Now, although there are various proclamations and laws to protect freedom, they cannot be effectively implemented due to the necessity of facts. In addition, due to the incompleteness of the law, the executors have no basis, and the entry and exit are light or heavy, losing their balance. The people feel the pain of freedom being arbitrarily restricted, and increasingly doubt the law on which the restrictors are based. The harms are as follows: (1) The people's freedom is not effectively guaranteed, and on the one hand, it is the government officials who have no clear responsibility, and the unscrupulous can use the cause as a pretext for wrongdoing. (2) Without effective protection of property, investors will stop and not move forward, and there will be no way for industry and commerce to develop. (3) Without the freedom of speech, publication, assembly, and association explicitly granted by law, public opinion cannot be expressed, and the power of the government will become empty. Reactionaries can use the suspicious psychology of the general public to take advantage of and spread rumors and incite. The above harms must be remedied in the following ways:

(1) Those who have set up methods to protect the freedom of the people in law should implement them effectively. There is more than one aspect of the law to protect freedom. The Civil Law, the Criminal Law, the Litigation Law, and all administrative laws and regulations were originally aimed at protecting freedom. Most of these laws have been promulgated and implemented. There are five concrete ways to promote implementation: A. The Central Party Department should issue orders to all subordinate party departments and party members to strictly prohibit actions that violate freedom without legal basis. At the same time, the National Government should issue orders to all administrative and judicial organs in the country that no people shall be arrested without following the procedures of the Police Law and the Criminal Procedure Law, and no freedom of property shall be infringed without following administrative laws and regulations (such as the Land Expropriation Law, etc.). If there are those who are instructed by party department party members, individuals, or mass organizations to illegally infringe on the freedom of person or property, the official in charge shall bear the responsibility himself. In addition to constituting a crime under ordinary criminal law, special criminal law shall be used to stipulate the method of punishment. B. The government should issue orders to mass organizations that, whether for their members or the people outside the organization, they shall not take actions that infringe on freedom without legal basis, and must absolutely comply with the sanctions of the law. C. Military organs, except during martial law, if there are actions to arrest people or harm the freedom of property, other laws shall be used to stipulate or amend the current laws and regulations to allow judicial organs to exercise their power of trial, and the government shall use effective methods to protect the judicial organs in exercising these powers. D. The National Government shall determine the judicial funding of the central and provincial governments, and shall stipulate laws to increase the powers of judicial organs, and shall formulate a law on court appearances to make the court responsible for effectively protecting the freedom of the people. E. The Administrative Litigation Law and the Organizational Law of the Administrative Court shall be formulated as soon as possible, and the Administrative Court shall be established immediately. The organization shall be based on the principle of facilitating the people to exercise administrative litigation.

(2) For those who have not formulated laws, the National Government must formulate them as soon as possible. There are several important parts concerning the freedom of the people that have not been formulated into laws: A. Publication, B. Association, C. Assembly. The above three laws shall be determined by the Political Conference to determine its principles, and handed over to the Legislative Yuan to formulate it within a time limit. Other administrative laws and regulations must also be sorted out strictly within a time limit. Combining the above effective implementation of the protection methods in the established law, the people's freedom can be fully protected. Is it appropriate? I respectfully await your public decision. Proposer: Chen Mingshu, co-signers: Liu Wendao, Zhu Jiahua, Wu Jingheng, Sun Ke, Wang Chonghui, Wang Boling, Yang Shuzhuang, Li Shizeng.

Proposal on Unified Management of Studying Abroad

Central Committee member Fang Juehui proposed a method for unifying the dispatch and management of students studying abroad, saying that the Ministry of Education and various provinces have set up public-funded quotas for studying abroad. Recently, the Central Party Department and the various departments and committees of the National Government have dispatched students to study abroad, and military commanders in the country have also privately sent students to study abroad. If this continues, if the central government does not thoroughly rectify the problem of studying abroad and unify the power to dispatch and manage it in the Central Party Department, the accumulated malpractices of studying abroad will become more and more serious, and the academic future will be unimaginable. Therefore, the following methods are proposed: (1) The central government shall establish a committee for the examination and management of studying abroad to be in charge of matters such as the examination and management of studying abroad. (2) All students who pass the entrance examination for studying abroad must be trained by the committee for three months to assess their interests and abilities. (3) The committee shall investigate the number of students to be sent abroad in the future, the funding, and the subjects to be entered. (4) Students to be sent abroad shall be subject to preliminary examination by the original dispatching agency and re-examination by the committee. The qualifications for the examination shall be determined separately, but revolutionary youths who have served in the party for more than six years may be assisted by other methods if their qualifications and level do not meet the requirements. (5) All national universities, in order to train specialized teachers, can be exempted from re-examination for sending professors at their own expense, but they only need to report to the committee for record. (6) The funding for studying abroad shall be borne by the original dispatching agency, and the committee shall review the amount and hand it over to the committee for remittance, so as to avoid delays and differences in treatment.

Proposal on the Central Government Recruiting Talents

Liu Zhi proposed to concentrate talents and enrich the central cadres to promote construction. Our party is responsible for building the country with the party, saving the country with the party, and governing the country with the party. When the Premier was in Japan, heroes from all directions followed the scenery, but it is still insufficient to build the country. In recent years, party cadres have sacrificed for the revolution. In addition, due to drastic changes in the situation, party cadres have been divided many times, and talents are becoming increasingly scarce. Now that the military campaign to suppress the rebellion is coming to an end, it is time to start anew with the people. We should do our best to recruit specialized talents from all over the country to enrich the various departments and offices of the central government to promote construction and shoulder difficult tasks.

Proposal on Establishing Special Administrative Regions

Lu Diping proposed the establishment of special administrative regions, saying, "In order to propose, I have investigated that the provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian have been repeatedly disturbed by bandits and Communists, and have suffered from burning, killing, and looting for a long time. The red atmosphere is pervasive, and the poison is deep. The bandit areas where bandits and Communists have occupied for the longest time, such as Liuyang and Pingjiang in eastern Hunan, Dayong and Sangzhi in western Hunan, Lianhua, Ninggang, and Yongxin in western Jiangxi, Donggu and Mobanshan in eastern Jiangxi, and Honghu in Hubei, have been mired in bandit lairs for a long time, and the people have also been deeply poisoned. The army's suppression can only eliminate a limited number of bandit troops. For these ignorant and coerced masses, it is too cruel to kill them, and it is endless to condone them. In order to prevent the embers from burning again and to eliminate the roots of bandits and Communists, the only way is to divide the areas that have suffered the longest and been the most deeply poisoned into special administrative regions, and strictly establish political organizations to fulfill the responsibility of supervision and management, and strengthen party affairs work to achieve the effect of training and transformation. After a considerable period of time, it can be restored to its original state. The outline for the establishment of special administrative regions is as follows:

Page 9

Receiving Important Domestic Telegrams

Left, (1) All areas that have been disturbed by bandits and Communists for more than one year shall be designated as special administrative regions. (2) The regulations and revocation of special administrative regions shall be ordered by the provincial governments of each province. (3) A special administrative region management committee shall be established as the highest administrative organ of the special administrative region, directly under the provincial government. (4) The number of members of the special administrative region management committee shall be determined by the provincial governments of each province on a temporary basis, taking into account the local conditions. However, in order to carefully organize this power organ, two-thirds of the members shall be proposed by the provincial government, one-third shall be proposed by the provincial party department, and one person shall be proposed by the higher court of each province and appointed by the provincial government. (5) All residents of the special administrative region shall have their civil rights suspended, except as otherwise ordered, but may be restored at any time with the permission of the special administrative region management committee. (6) All administration of the special administrative region shall not be subject to the constraints of ordinary laws, but shall be reported to the provincial government for approval and implementation at any time. Whether the above is appropriate,

I respectfully await your public decision.

Proposal to Revise the Provincial Administrative Regions

Commissioner Chen Mingshu proposed a proposal to revise the principles of provincial administrative regions (co-signed by ten commissioners including Hu Hanmin). The original text is as follows:

Our country has a vast territory, and governance is difficult. The Republic of China was founded, and all undertakings were renewed, but the division of administrative regions still followed the old provincial system since the Yuan Dynasty. The malpractices are that the upper level cannot be governed by the central government, and the lower level cannot be solely responsible for the local government, and the situation of warlords occupying territory has become a desire to remedy its evils, mostly based on the view of inheritance, and advocated the theory of the joint provincial autonomy, which is to make the occupation of territory a theoretical basis, and to give the warlords institutional protection. Only the Premier saw through its crux, and advocated raising the status of the county, and the province was only established between the central government and the county, to collect its contact effect. The essence of the Premier's entire nation-building program, on the exercise of governance, lies in this. If we base on the Premier's遗教 and make practical facilities, then the provincial area must be re-revised. The current provincial area of our country, the size of one province is almost the same as one country, with the protection of the army, and the power to manipulate finance, it has become the foundation for the generation of warlords. If the provincial area is reduced, and the provincial power is reduced, then even if the warlords have the heart to occupy, there is no place to occupy. Also, if the provincial area is too large, the supervision of the county's self-government by the governor is not easy to be meticulous, the status of the county is too low, and the local administration is inconvenient due to multiple twists and turns, local administration cannot be measured and used in the construction of the county's self-government, if the provincial area is reduced, and the provincial power is reduced, then the self-government is easier to complete. The size of one province is almost the same as one country, then the talent to govern the province must be the talent to govern the country, the talent is concentrated in the central government and there is more than enough, and scattered to the provinces is not enough, so the central government and the provinces all feel the pain of the difficulty of talent, and the talent to govern the province is not enough, and used to govern the county, or there is more than enough, the provincial area is reduced, and the provincial power is reduced, then the talent who is superior to governing the province is concentrated in the central government, and the talent who is not enough to govern the province is scattered to the counties, and the talent is enough. As for the method of revising the provincial area, it is based on the old Dao area as the standard, the division of the old Dao area is mostly based on historical habits, the shape of mountains and rivers, and the size is moderate and convenient to adopt, but there are special circumstances such as the convenience of economic development, the adjustment of poor and rich areas, etc., which will be determined by the central government separately. As for the provincial use of the provincial governor system and the duties of the provincial governor, the Outline for Nation Building has a general provision, and the division of central finance and local finance is especially cautious. In this way, the government can avoid the disadvantages of a huge organization and stacking beds on the roof. At this time of suppressing the rebellion and achieving unification, the rapid completion of self-government, and the prevention of the re-emergence of warlords, the only important task is to earnestly implement the legacy shown by the Premier's Outline for Nation Building. I have listed the principles as far as I can see, and if they are adopted, please ask the Central Political Conference to detail the methods, and hand it over to the Legislative Yuan to formulate the New Provincial Law for implementation. Is it appropriate? Please make a public decision.

Principles (1) Revise the current provincial area, and use the old Dao area as the provincial area, but if there are special circumstances, it shall be determined separately by the central government. (2) A governor shall be established in the province, appointed by the central government, and at the beginning of the constitutional government period, the governor shall be elected by the National Assembly in accordance with the Outline for Nation Building. (3) Abolish the current Organizational Law of the Provincial Government, and separately formulate the Organizational Regulations of the Provincial Governor's Office. (4) The administrative expenses of the Provincial Governor's Office shall be paid by the central government. (5) The duties of the governor are to supervise the local self-government of the counties within the province, and the national administration within the province shall be subject to the command of the central government. (6) After the provincial system is formulated according to the above principles, the central and county tax revenue shall all follow the division of Article 11 of the Outline for Nation Building, and the county's burden on the central government shall be verified according to the circumstances of each county.

Proposal to Amend the Regulations of the Political Conference

Sun Ke proposed to amend the regulations of the Central Political Conference. The original text is as follows:

(Reason) The Central Political Conference is the highest guiding organ for implementing political tutelage throughout the country. The matters stipulated to be discussed and resolved are the Outline for Nation Building, legislative principles, administrative policy, military grand strategy, financial plan, and the selection of various political officials, although it does not directly issue orders and handle political affairs, but it is actually the central hub of the national political movement, and it is precious to use it flexibly and command quickly, and then the political affairs can be promoted, and the effect of the body using the arm and the arm using the finger can be achieved. However, after observing the past years, there are important grand strategies concerning the administration of various departments that should be decided by the central government, but the Political Conference has not yet been involved. There are also major plans of various departments that have been submitted to the Political Conference through the Executive Yuan, but because the heads of the various departments are not central members, they cannot attend the meeting, so the various members cannot deeply understand the case, so they hastily decide or directly hand it over to the various groups to put it aside for a long time. After the case has been handed over to the group for review, the original proposing organ has no one to attend the explanation, and temporary invitations are often inconvenient, so even after review, it cannot be properly resolved, and it often happens. All of these have lost the original intention of the central government to use the Political Conference to promote politics, and must be remedied urgently. (Method) The way to remedy it is that the heads of all central departments and committees in the future, even if they are not central members, should also be allowed to attend the Political Conference, limited to the ministers and vice ministers of the various departments and the chairmen and vice chairmen of the various committees. In this way, the various barriers between the central government and the heads of the various departments and committees can be eliminated, and it will be easier to get a clue and quickly resolve the various matters under discussion. As for the various groups established under the Political Conference, the ministers of the various departments and the chairmen of the various committees can be made to participate in them, so as to jointly undertake the work of review and design of various items. The vice ministers or vice chairmen of the various departments can be made to concurrently serve as special secretaries of the various groups, and they must be more familiar with the ins and outs of the various cases than others, and it is convenient to handle them, easy to consult, and ask. This method is of great help to the politics of party transformation. The responsibility of our party is to use the power of the party to promote politics, which is certainly necessary. If you agree to the public decision, please submit the current regulations of the Central Political Conference for amendment, so as to facilitate movement and benefit progress. The party and the country are fortunate. Whether all the reasons and methods for amending the regulations of the Central Political Conference are feasible, I respectfully await your public decision.

Sun Lianzhong Talks About the Mission of This Trip to Nanjing

Discussing matters such as pacification and defense zones

(Nanjing) Sun Lianzhong said that this trip is to discuss various matters related to pacification and defense zones. He will return to his post after everything is settled. A portion of his troops has been transferred to suppress bandits in western Shandong, but this requires consultation with the Shandong Provincial Government before they can be dispatched. The remaining troops are still stationed in Xinxiang on the Daokou-Qinghua Railway. The organizational structure of the troops is still the old system, currently divided into four mixed brigades and two mixed cavalry brigades. They are waiting to receive the Central Government's organizational chart before reorganizing, and they will also request the Central Government to send personnel to inspect. (14th Dispatch)

The Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee to Meet at the Judicial Yuan Today

(Nanjing) The Internal and External Debt Consolidation Committee is scheduled to convene a meeting with representatives of various creditor nations at the Judicial Yuan at 2:00 PM on the 15th. Expected attendees include representatives of creditor nations such as England, France, the United States, Italy, Japan, Belgium, Denmark, Sweden, and the Netherlands, as well as Chinese committee members Wang Chonghui, Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, Song Ziwen, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Boqun, and Zhang Xueliang. The total amount of internal and external debt is 2 billion yuan, with the ratio of internal to external debt being 12 to 8.

(Nanjing) The conference on the consolidation of internal and external debt is still being held in Nanjing. The chairman of the Consolidation Committee, originally Tan Yankai, has now been replaced by Wang Chonghui. Leaders of foreign banking groups in Peiping and the banking community in Tianjin have arrived in Nanjing one after another. It is said that on the 13th, committee members Song Ziwen, Sun Ke, Wang Zhengting, and Wang Boqun, as well as Secretary-General Zeng Rongfu, were invited by Wang Chonghui to the Judicial Yuan for a discussion on the consolidation plan. Zhang Xueliang also participated. (14th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The communist bandits on the west bank of the Gan River retreated without a fight. On the 10th, Zhu De and Mao Zedong fled eastward to Chongren, attempting to disturb Linchuan. Danger threatened. On the 12th, the Zhang and Tan divisions advanced from Fengcheng and Qingjiang to Chongren and Fuzhou overnight, forming a pincer attack with the Deng division. According to a telegram from County Magistrate Wang of Linchuan, Zhu De and Peng Dehuai retreated to Yihuang when they saw our troops arrive. Airplanes have been flying over the Chongren area for days, bombing and killing many communist bandits. Fuzhou has turned from danger to safety. (13th Dispatch)

Foreign Important Telegrams

Japanese Prime Minister Hamaguchi Suddenly Attacked

Bullet Hits Lower Abdomen, Not Yet Fatal

Assailant Sagoya Arrested on the Spot

Condition Good After Surgery

Rumors of Binhara Assuming Temporary Regency

Motive for Assassination Allegedly Due to Economic Recession

▲Japanese Associated Press, Tokyo, 14th: Prime Minister Hamaguchi was shot in the abdomen by a strong man at Tokyo Station at 8:50 AM this morning while on his way to inspect the Okayama Army Grand Maneuvers. The assailant was arrested on the spot.

▲Dentsu, Tokyo, 14th: The assassination attempt on Prime Minister Hamaguchi occurred precisely when the special express train bound for the west was departing at 9:00 AM. There were many people seeing him off at the station. The newly appointed Ambassador to Moscow, Hirota, was also on the same train as the Prime Minister, so the station was very crowded. The sound of the gunshot was indistinguishable from the sound of cameras taking pictures, and even those nearby did not notice. Only when the Prime Minister fell to the ground did people realize what had happened and panic. The perpetrator, Sagoya Tomeo, was wearing a plain white cotton kimono, a dark blue pleated skirt, and wooden clogs. He approached the Prime Minister from the crowd of well-wishers and took out a concealed handgun to shoot him, causing great chaos at Tokyo Station.

▲Dentsu, Tokyo, 14th: After being shot, Hamaguchi immediately fainted. He was carried to the stationmaster's office and given emergency treatment. The bullet hit his thigh, but did not pass through completely. It stopped between his thigh and lower abdomen. The peritoneum and intestines were severely injured, and the Prime Minister seemed to be in considerable pain. Fortunately, he was still conscious and able to speak with Secretary Nakajima. Later, the bleeding increased, and he could not be moved. It is currently impossible to say whether his life is in danger. The assailant is being interrogated by Inspector Nakamura of the Hibiya Police Station. According to his confession, he is Sagoya Tomeo, 23 years old, from Nagasaki Prefecture, and is lodging at the home of Yoshikatsu Matsumoto. He wanted to assassinate the Prime Minister to restore the economic situation and had no accomplices. His motive for the crime and whether he has any connections are currently unknown.

▲Dentsu: Regarding Sagoya's military service status, the Nagasaki Prefecture Military Affairs Section announced that Sagoya underwent a conscription examination in Akasaka Ward, Tokyo, in the 3rd year of Showa (1928). Although he was a graduate of an ordinary elementary school, he was considered to have completed two years of middle school at the time of the examination. From this point of view, he seems to have studied hard to some extent. He is 5 feet 1.9 inches tall, weighs 59 kilograms, and was deemed fit for Category C service. According to the family register, the perpetrator is an illegitimate child from Oshima Village, Kitamatsuura County, Nagasaki Prefecture, born on December 1, Meiji 41 (1908). Because he could not enter his mother's family, he established his own family and registered on December 7 of that year. His mother, Isoko, became pregnant with Tomeo when she was a geisha in Sonogi Village in the 40th year of Meiji (1907), through an affair with a certain Mr. Tsuchikata. Tsuchikata later disappeared, and Tomeo was born.

According to the Japanese Associated Press, the assailant who shot Prime Minister Hamaguchi, Sagoya Tomeo, was born in Gyeongseong (Seoul), Korea. His father runs a woodworking business in Sogane-cho, Gyeongseong, and has some wealth. Tomeo graduated from an elementary school in Gyeongseong and has always had a violent temperament and strong class consciousness. At the age of seventeen, he worked under Cheongi (bandit chieftain) in Manchuria. He returned to mainland Japan once in the 10th year of Taisho (1921) and then immediately returned to Manchuria to work as a bandit between Tanigawa and Cheongi. At the age of twenty, he returned to mainland Japan to Tokyo, and often frequented political and educational societies and national language societies. He became a member of the Patriotic Society this June. Although he does not drink alcohol, his nature is violent. He was charged with affray and assault on January 3rd of last year and August 15th of this year, and is currently still serving a three-month suspended sentence.

▲Dentsu, Tokyo, 14th: Party leaders and others rushed to Tokyo Station after receiving news of the Prime Minister's assassination. Because his condition was dangerous, all visits were prohibited. Afterwards, Dr. Hayashi, Dr. Shioda, and Dr. Kondo jointly consulted on the Prime Minister's wound and determined that he needed absolute rest and should be injected with Ringer's solution. At the same time, about 190 grams of blood were injected from the Prime Minister's second son, Iwane, which slightly restored his energy. After Dr. Shioda performed surgery at 1:15 PM, Dr. Shioda announced the procedure as follows: The bullet entered the abdomen 3 cm below the navel, passed through six places in the upper part of the jejunum, and after the mesentery of the descending colon, it entered the left buttocks from the abdominal wall. During the surgery, 50 cm of the jejunum was cut off, the blood that had overflowed into the abdominal cavity was removed, the peritoneum was cleaned, and an eggplant-induced method was performed. The surgery ended at 2:00 PM. During the surgery, the pulse was good, and the spirit was clear. He talked to people from time to time. Based on experience during the European War, patients with this type of injury can survive if they can last for more than ten hours.

▲Dentsu: Regarding the Prime Minister Hamaguchi's condition and progress, either a temporary cabinet meeting will be held, or a temporary prime minister will be appointed. At that time, Foreign Minister Shidehara may concurrently serve as temporary prime minister.

Disarmament Conference Continues Discussion on Army Armament Limitation Proposal

German and French Representatives Engage in Heated Debate; Italy Proposes Amending British Proposal

▲Guomin News Agency, Geneva, 13th: The Disarmament Preparatory Commission has been discussing for three days whether to directly or indirectly limit army armaments (indirect restriction means limiting the budget). No clear results have been achieved. A final vote on the resolution proposed by British representative Cecil will have to wait until Friday. Today, only the first two sections and the provisions regarding armaments were barely passed. Today's debate was dominated by the heated exchange between the German and French representatives. In addition, the Italian representative proposed amending the Cecil proposal, arguing that the most effective limitation of armaments must be considered on both direct and indirect fronts.

Strikes in Peru, Student Riots in Cuba

▲Reuters, Lima, Peru, 13th: A dispute has arisen here between the owner of a British-owned textile factory and the workers, resulting in a general strike in Peru's main industrial center. ▲Reuters, New York, 14th: According to news from Havana, Cuba, six people have died and seventy-two have been injured in riots in the past seventy-two hours. Martial law has been declared in the city. Soldiers patrol the streets, and residents do not go out. All newspapers except the government gazette have suspended publication to protest censorship. In early October, the Senate approved President Machado's request to suspend constitutional guarantees in Havana and its four surrounding districts until the general election on November 1. Constitutional guarantees are the various freedoms of speech and assembly enjoyed by the people. Suspending this right is tantamount to declaring a disguised form of martial law.

Domestic Important News

Latest Developments in the Longjing Village Case

▲Reports of Japanese Police Retreating from Yanbian

Jilin News Agency: After the unfortunate incident in Longjing Village, Yanbian, on the 6th of last month due to Japanese police provocation, the Japanese side immediately seized the opportunity to deploy 106 armed Japanese police officers from the Korean border to Longbu, harassing various parts of Yanbian and doing whatever they pleased. The people of Yanbian repeatedly appealed to all parties and held a citizens' meeting to urge the Japanese side to realize their wrongdoing. The Jilin Provincial Government, considering the matter to be related to international relations, reported to Liaoning, which telegraphed the central government to protest to the Japanese ambassador. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs also engaged in serious negotiations with Acting Ambassador Shigemitsu, but received no reply, and the situation in Yanbian became increasingly serious. Therefore, it ordered local officials to negotiate on the spot. Subsequently, Zhang Shuhan, the head of the Yanji Municipal Preparatory Office and in charge of negotiations, and Okada, the Japanese Consul-General of Jiandao, held several rounds of talks. The Japanese side was initially very tough, and at the same time made representations to Chairman Zhang in Liaoning, demanding compensation, punishment of the perpetrators, apology, and guarantees. After our side replied that the Japanese police must first be withdrawn before considering accommodating them within a possible scope, the Japanese side also showed some concession. Therefore, on the morning of the 5th of this month, all the above-mentioned Japanese police officers were withdrawn to Korea, and negotiations continued with us in order to reach a quick resolution. Currently, it is in progress. It is reported that the Japanese side initially proposed 40,000 yuan for the pensions of the two Japanese police officers killed and some medical expenses for the injured Japanese police officer, but it has now been reduced to 10,000 yuan. Both sides have also made concessions on other conditions, but the details are kept secret by the authorities and will probably only be announced after everything is completed. (November 8th)

Communist Bandits in Jiangxi Province Collapsing and Retreating in Different Directions

▲Fang and Shao's Gang Flee to the Anhui Border ▲Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang Flee to Eastern Jiangxi

▲Anhui Province to Join the Suppression ▲Jiangxi Army Pursues Towards Fuzhou

Nanchang News Agency: The three provinces of Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei have already launched a large-scale campaign to suppress the Communist bandits. Recently, Anhui has also joined, changing it to a four-province joint suppression, which is still commanded by He Chengjun as the Commander-in-Chief of the Suppression of Bandits in the Four Provinces. The reason is that the Communist gangs of Fang Zhimin and Shao Shiping have been harassing the northeast of Jiangxi and the border areas of Anhui and Hubei, such as Wuyuan and Susong, so Anhui Province has joined the suppression in order to eliminate them. According to reports, the Communist leader Fang Zhimin in eastern Jiangxi recently attempted to purchase firearms from a foreign merchant ship on Pengze Lake in northern Jiangxi, but was defeated by the naval fleet at Hukou and retreated to eastern Jiangxi. Currently, most of Fang's bandits are still entrenched in the towns of Dexing, Jingzhen, Leping, and the countryside of Raozhou and Duchang, propagating communism. The people of each village have fled, and the county magistrates and representatives of each county in eastern Jiangxi, such as Jiang Bozhang, have separately requested Chairman Lu in Nanxun and Hu Zuyu to send troops to suppress them. In addition to telegraphing the Chairman of Anhui to send Yue Shengxuan's troops to the Jiangxi border as soon as possible, Lu also ordered Hu Zuyu to advance from northern Jiangxi to eastern Jiangxi to implement a joint suppression. It is reported that Yue's troops have already set out from Wuyuan to the Dexing area, and Hu's troops have also ordered the 28th and 29th Regiments to advance from Pengze Lake to Jingzhen and Duchang.

As for the gangs of Peng, Huang, Zhu, and Mao, their main force, the so-called 1st, 3rd, 5th, 8th, 12th, and 20th Pseudo-Armies, originally gathered in Xinyu, Fenyi, Qingjiang south of the Yuan River, and Anfu, Xiajiang, Jishui, Ji'an, and Xingan west of the Gan River. They claimed to have 100,000 men, but only had 20,000 to 30,000 rifles. Each rifle had less than two rows of bullets. The rest were a rabble of peasant bandits, either unarmed or with spears. Lu Dipin, the Commander-in-Chief of the Nine Route Armies, had already ordered the 18th, 50th, 20th, New 13th, and 77th Divisions to advance fiercely towards Qingjiang and Xinyu. As soon as the general offensive order was issued, the four counties of Qingjiang, Xingan, Xinyu, and Fenyi were recovered. Most of Zhu, Mao, Peng, and Huang crossed the Gan River from Xiajiang, passed through Yongfeng and Le'an, and fled to Fuzhou. According to news from Fuzhou, Chongren has already fallen, and Linchuan is also very critical. On the 10th, the city gates were tightly closed and a special curfew was imposed. The boats gathered west of the Fu River were all hoisted to the eastern bank of Xijingdu to cut off traffic. Many people have fled to the province from Fuzhou in the past two days, and there are rumors that Fuzhou is difficult to defend. However, since the day before yesterday, the 1st and 5th Aviation Squadrons have been departing for Chongren in the rain to bomb the bandits. According to report No. 53 of Kesa, Communist bandits were discovered near Chong City on the 11th, and six 120-pound bombs were dropped, all of which exploded, killing many bandits. Recently, Mao Bingwen's troops, which had been concentrated in the provincial capital, also advanced towards Fuzhou at full speed. At the same time, the Zhang and Tan troops in Fengcheng and Qingjiang are closely pursuing the bandits from the east of the Gan River towards Chongren and Le'an, and will join forces with Deng Ying's division in Fuzhou to attack them from both sides. Therefore, the Communist bandits will likely flee from Guangchang to the Fujian border.

Commander-in-Chief Lu immediately issued a commendation order to the Zhang and Luo divisions for recapturing the four counties of Xinyu, etc., and also telegraphed the commanders of each column to advance at full speed. The situation of Luo's division recapturing Fenyi has been reported to the province, with the text saying, "This morning, our Yi Brigade led its troops from Fengyang Bridge to suppress the Communist bandits occupying Jieqiao and Fenyi. The bandits in Jieqiao immediately fled to the southeast. The main force in Fenyi did not know that our army was advancing rapidly. When our main force arrived at the city, they began to resist. After about two hours of street fighting, our Hu Brigade joined in from the right wing, and the bandit troops could not resist, and fled in panic to the south bank of the Yuan River. In this battle, about 200 bandits were killed, and more than 400 bandits were captured alive, including a commander, Wei. Two puppet regimental commanders, Li Shucai and Li Jufeng, and the Chairman of the Soviet, Qiu Weidao, were drowned. We captured more than 200 rifles, spears, flags, and baggage, and Pseudo-Army Commander Huang Gonglue and Pseudo-Division Commander Long Zidao are on the run. More than ten members of our troops were injured. Details will be reported later. Sincerely, Luo Lin." (November 12th)

Local News

Songjiang

Re-discussion of Winter Rent Quality and Reduction: The quality of this year's rent collection has been previously agreed upon by various public groups at 85%. Now, the county political meeting considers that the autumn harvest this year is the best in decades, with a maximum yield of three dan of rice per mu. When the supply of new grain ran out this year, the price of rice was 20 yuan per dan, which was also the highest in decades. It is considered excessive to collect three dan of rice per mu as a standard. In order to determine a moderate method, it has been decided that the rent collection quality for 1919 will be uniformly 81%, that is, 1.9 dou of rice will be exempted for every one dan of regular rent. The county government will reply to the county party headquarters in a letter, seek consent, and then announce its implementation. It is reported that the San Shan Tang rent collection office will also automatically reduce the rent and is said to be collecting at 80%.

Provincial Committee Guides People's Organizations: The Provincial Party Department has sent Zhang Renjie, the fourth district instructor, to organize people's organizations. Construction County has also sent Pei Dingxiang. Both arrived in Songjiang yesterday and convened a party and government talk meeting at the County Party Department to discuss matters. It was decided that both the party and government will jointly issue a notice explaining the importance and procedures of organizing people's organizations. The head of the training department of the Party Department and the head of the relevant section of the county government will jointly be responsible for guiding the organization. Regarding the reorganization of the County Chamber of Commerce, the party and government will jointly guide the old chamber of commerce in accordance with the organization procedures and regulations of the people's organizations, convene a meeting at the county government to discuss the organization of trade associations, and establish them all within two months.

Ministry of Education Orders Overseas Chinese Schools in Southeast Asia to Use Domestic Textbooks and Teaching Materials

▲Investigating Restrictions by Local Governments

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education instructed consuls in British and Dutch territories in Southeast Asia to investigate the restrictions imposed by local governments on the use of books in overseas Chinese schools. The original order stated, "The colonial governments of British and Dutch territories in Southeast Asia often impose unreasonable restrictions on textbooks and teaching materials used in overseas Chinese schools. Recently, it has been heard that these governments are even compiling, printing, and distributing textbooks themselves, and forcing overseas Chinese schools to adopt them. Their intention is nothing more than to anesthetize and weaken our youth and our overseas Chinese so that they can be driven and humiliated and become obedient subjects of imperialism without realizing it. Their intentions are extremely insidious. However, the methods used by these governments to restrict textbooks and the contents of the textbooks they compile should be collected and studied to serve as a basis for negotiations. Please collect this information from nearby locations and send it to the Ministry quickly for verification. Also, please inform the overseas Chinese schools under your jurisdiction to freely adopt the textbooks and teaching materials approved by the Ministry and reject the textbooks compiled and printed by these governments. This is extremely important." This order.

Ministry of Education Orders Liaoning Province to Investigate Manchurian Textbooks

The Ministry of Education is urgently seeking to investigate the contents of Manchurian textbooks compiled by Japanese-run schools in Manchuria in order to prevent their conspiracy of aggression. Yesterday, the Ministry ordered the Education Department of Liaoning Province to collect and send the Manchurian textbooks from nearby locations to the Ministry for reference. The original order stated, "The 'Manchurian Readers' used by Japanese schools along the South Manchurian Railway extensively draw materials from Manchuria's local customs, human conditions, and social conditions. Their compilation methods are also different from the textbooks commonly used in Japan. The Ministry now intends to collect these textbooks in order to study them in detail, prevent the Japanese conspiracy of aggression, and provide reference for compiling Southeast Asian readers. The Education Department should find ways to obtain a complete set of these textbooks as easily as possible and send them to the Ministry quickly.

The pure youths will be further inspired by Mr. Yu, and the youths who have been numbed will also be guided by Mr. Yu and turn back. Chairman and Professors of the Agricultural College of Labor University Reply to Li Lianggong

A letter from the Chairman and Professors of the Agricultural College of Labor University to President Li Lianggong reads: "President Lianggong, Greetings. In recent days, newspapers have been filled with students' 'declarations' and 'warnings,' lengthy articles that specifically attack Mr. Fang Cheng, Mr. Wu Shuge, and Mr. Chen Guorong. This tactic of divide and conquer has been your sole weapon in dealing with your colleagues for the past month. We know that your intention is to expand the student unrest in order to overthrow the school affairs committee, hoping to become acting president, and then to change from acting to official president to achieve your grand goal. Yesterday, we read your letter to the faculty and staff of the Agricultural College. Everything that was in the students' declaration was also present in your letter, as if you were confessing that you were the mastermind behind this student unrest. You revealed the truth yourself, and now the truth is clear to the world. In the past, we did not hesitate to advance or retreat for personal reasons, and we did not dare to speak frankly in order to seek social judgment. However, at a time when our school is in turmoil, it cannot withstand further damage. Therefore, we have tried our best to tolerate and avoid disputes with students. We also know that once the academic atmosphere of the school is destroyed by careerists, it will be difficult for those who come later to clean up. Therefore, we are especially unwilling to use our pens to create a situation of multiple litigations, which would give you an opportunity to take advantage of. Now that you have bothered to fill the paper with slander, how can we not refute it? (1) You said that there are three major points of contention at this school. The first is that the entire student body opposes the school affairs committee and tricked Mr. Peng Xiang and Mr. Cheng Ganyun into leaving. The second is that the students of the Chemistry Department oppose Mr. Fang Cheng and Mr. Wu Shuge. The third is that the students of the Horticulture Department oppose Mr. Chen Guorong. Regarding the first point, we will leave it to the colleagues of the school affairs committee and Mr. Peng and Mr. Cheng to answer, and we will not waste words. However, the school affairs committee was originally something you wanted to control and manipulate. Now that you want to overthrow it, isn't that strange? Before the third meeting of the school affairs committee, you sent a telegram to prevent all the professor representatives from the Agricultural College from attending, hoping to cause a quorum to fail. Before the fourth meeting of the school affairs committee, at midnight, you knocked on Mr. Fang Cheng's door and told him, 'Tomorrow, we will propose a motion to impeach the temporary administrative committee and a motion to approve the appointment of the president. Our Agricultural College representatives have nine votes. Combined with Xiong Zirong and Zhang Ba's votes, we only have eleven votes. If we can sway three people to remain neutral, we can win.' On the day of the meeting, Mr. Fang Cheng was unable to attend due to other business. You then brazenly appointed Mr. Zhu Tongjiu to serve as a representative. All of these are facts of your conspiracy to manipulate the school affairs committee. Even if you are as good at disguise as you are, you may not have a word to say. After the remote meeting was opened, the Agricultural College representatives were deeply disgusted by your base methods, completely treating the professor representatives as personal tools. Furthermore, because this meeting was very important to the future of the school, the majority opposed your proposal. From then on, you regarded the school affairs committee as a thorn in your side, and you had to remove it before you could be happy. You immediately changed your battle plan and actively incited student unrest. Furthermore, because of the failure at this meeting, due to the refusal of the Agricultural College representatives to agree with your personal plans, the Horticulture Department students suddenly attacked Mr. Chen the day after the meeting, and the Chemistry Department students suddenly attacked Mr. Fang and Mr. Wu. Mr. Chen, Mr. Fang, and Mr. Wu are not present as representatives of the school, and you believe that in order to shoot someone, you must shoot the horse first. (To be continued)"
