Report matters: (1) The Ministry's instruction to the Directorate General to cancel the rice subsidy for Shanghai Bureau employees. (2) The Municipal Party Committee's instruction has been forwarded to the Shanghai Postal Administration to reinstate Wang Fusheng's position. (3) The case of the two committee members Shui Xiangyun and Xing Rongzhao being stationed at the union office has been negotiated with the authorities and a response will be received soon. (4) The autoworker Yan Jiajun requested an investigation into whether there was an error and requested protection. The investigation department has conducted extensive investigations, but it is currently difficult to determine the truth. (5) The deliverymen's winter greatcoats will be issued slightly later this winter because domestic goods are being used. They should be issued in about two weeks. (6) The coolies on the night shift at the yard requested extra work at 1.5 jiao per hour. This has been negotiated with the authorities. The postmaster has accepted the principle, but statistics must be added before it can be announced. (7) The revised year-end bonus case has been approved by the Ministry and will be implemented this year. Discussion matters: (1) How should the issue of demanding the dismissal of Liu Shufan continue? It was decided to send a representative to the Municipal Party Committee to request that it be forwarded to the Fourth Plenary Session. (2) Announce the union's firm stance and actively cooperate with the labor unions. (2) Zhu Xuefan resigned from the Standing Committee of the All-China Postal Union. It was decided to approve the resignation and appoint Zhao Shusheng as his successor. However, Zhu Xuefan will act as an agent during Zhao Shusheng's long leave. (3) The twenty-ninth branch proposed that the authorities order the letter carriers to pay for the repair or replace parts on schedule for damaged bicycles, which is unfair. The investigation department has investigated the case, how should it be handled? It was decided to request the authorities to stipulate that if it is damaged during the bicycle's usage period and ordered to be compensated, then those that are overdue should be given bonuses, and the negotiation department should negotiate the handling. (5) The tenth branch proposed that the current rice subsidy has been cancelled, and it is difficult for extra servants to make a living. It is requested that a subsidy of six yuan per month be given. It was decided to reply by letter. (6) The tenth branch proposed that coolies who have worked for three years can participate in special examinations, and those who have worked for ten years can be promoted to servants without conditions. It was decided to reply by letter. (7) The fifth branch's autoworkers requested that shoes and socks be treated the same as letter carriers. It was decided that the reasons were insufficient and it was difficult to handle. The secretary's office should reply by letter. (8) The second branch presented that since the beginning of winter, the weather has been cold, and the hot water radiators in the bureau are only on from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM, and night shift workers cannot keep warm. It should be requested that the negotiation be handled. It was decided that the water radiators are now on from 9:00 AM to 9:00 PM, and the request does not need to be discussed. (9) The second branch proposed that the addresses on registered return receipts are often unclear, making it impossible to deliver them. It should be requested to negotiate with the authorities to improve them to benefit the people and facilitate delivery. It was decided to send a letter to the postmaster. (10) The Supervisory Committee requested to prepare office supplies for the union office. It was decided to purchase a writing desk. (11) The executive and supervisory badges have been made, can they be adopted? It was decided to approve the adoption. (12) The Overseas Chinese Federation sent a letter to the union requesting that it jointly launch a campaign to convene a conference to aid Xiao (Xin'an). How should it be handled? It was decided that the standing committee members should be responsible for participating.

▲ Ship and Timber Union The Ship and Timber Union held its ninth executive and supervisory joint meeting yesterday, chaired by Ye Xianggao, recorded by Chen Binwu. The ceremony was conducted as usual. Matters decided: (1) The draft of the Labor Affairs Committee should be sent to the Standing Committee's review committee for review as soon as possible. (5) The previous strike period in Chedaijiao used the cost of the first branch to subsidize the case. It was decided to hand it over to the first branch's representative assembly for resolution. The rest were omitted.

▲ Acknowledgement We received the English Weekly No. 776, Nature Vol. 5 No. 8, and Children's World Vol. 26 No. 15 from the Commercial Press yesterday. We are grateful and would like to express our thanks.

Letter

Dear Sir, Yesterday I read your newspaper's local news column about Zhenhua Garden owner Li Guohua's accusation against Wu Rongchang for failing to deliver the ordered goods. The content of the report does not match the facts. I will now briefly describe the course of events below, hoping that you will correct it as a prayer. In March of this year, a street vendor from our company indirectly introduced Mr. Li, who brought a package of rubber samples and claimed that they were German products, and entrusted Xinji Foreign Company to order 10 tons, with a limited price of 98 yuan and 405 taels per ton. Because we had never traded with Mr. Li before, we collected a deposit of 400 yuan. After the sample arrived in Germany, it was said that the goods were not produced there. When the German rubber sample was sent back, Mr. Li said that it did not match. At that time, we verbally cancelled the order, but Mr. Li said that he still had a bag of previous goods, so we could find out the place of origin. Therefore, we did not get the deposit back. When we saw the words "BOWBAY" printed on the bag, we found that it was Indian goods. Mr. Li then entrusted Xinji to order from that country, but there was no news yet. Mr. Li went to Xinji and said that he had found out that the goods were actually produced in Little Luzon. Xinji was entrusted to send a letter, but it was not a product of that place, and the deposit was returned. Mr. Li seemed to be honest and did not say anything unexpected. He was instigated by an intermediary, which led to this unexpected move, which is also Mr. Li's misfortune. Xinji Limited Company, a British company, November 14th.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

▲ A (Giving a cloud cigar to B) - How is the flavor of this cigar that I gave you?

B (Lights it up, takes a puff) - Ugh. The flavor is terrible. Why do you smoke such a low-grade cigar?

A - You should ask yourself. Because this cigar is exactly the one you gave me the day before yesterday.

▲ Wife (Wakes up in the middle of the night from the bed, pushes her husband violently) - Dear, wake up quickly! Wake up quickly! The alarm has been ringing for a while. The sky is full of red light. I'm afraid the whole city is on fire!

Husband (Yawns and gets up, slowly gets out of bed, feels the four walls, and then goes back to bed and lies down) - Don't make such a fuss. The four walls are still cold. Besides, our accounts are not on fire either.

▲ Judge (To the criminal) - You have admitted that you sneaked into that house through the back door at half past twelve last night. What did you sneak in for?

Criminal - I thought that house was my own house.

Judge - If so, when the mistress of the house heard the noise and came to check, why did you hide under the bed in the attic?

Criminal - I thought my wife was coming. Because I have always been afraid of her shrewishness. It's always like this.

▲ Woman - My love, you must come to my house tonight. I'm waiting for you.

Man - But I'm most afraid of that old man in your garden. He's staring at me with his eyes wide open.

Woman - Don't pay attention to him. He's just my father.

Two Days After the Reading Movement

— Yan Qian

On the first day of the reading movement, Mr. Hu already had an article on the reading movement published in this talk. Now, I will show the reader the main points of the speeches of Mr. Chen Zhongfan and Mr. Wang Yunwu, the two speakers in the following two days, so that he can get a glimpse of the whole picture.

▲ Extend it a little in reverse According to the program scheduled by the Youth Association, the speaker on the second day should have been Wang Yunwu. However, because Mr. Wang was attending the Industrial and Commercial Conference in the capital, he was elected as the drafter of the declaration and could not rush back. So, Chen Zhongfan was temporarily asked to advance his speech by one day. When the author went to the meeting at three o'clock the next day, he saw a temporary notice at the door saying that Mr. Wang's speech had to be postponed to six o'clock. He asked the administrative office for the reason. They said that Mr. Wang would arrive in Shanghai from the capital, probably after three o'clock, or even after five o'clock. Mr. Wang did arrive at six o'clock and said that as soon as he got off the car, he was pulled over by people from the meeting. Although he had entered his home, it only took thirty seconds and he had not even had dinner. It is because Mr. Wang knows that more than a thousand young people are waiting in the hall for teaching while hungry. Speakers and listeners are all engaged in hunger, which is also a good story in the academic world.

▲ What books does Mr. Chen read Mr. Chen Zhongfan's topic was "What books to read." He divided all the books in the country into large categories of historical, philosophical, and literary, and discussed them in detail. There were many unique insights, such as the saying that Wang Fuzhi once advocated nationalism, Wang Zongyi once advocated democracy, and Gu Yanwu once advocated the people's livelihood. He also said that there is no special history in this country, such as the history of education and the history of art. Therefore, people who initially want to study a specialized subject often have a sigh that they have nowhere to start. However, all records contain a lot of special historical materials. If you can find them by category, you can get very good special historical materials in two or three months. Mr. also earnestly told people that reading must lay a good foundation in basic science, especially the study of academic must have a mathematical geometry and other foundations. When Mr. spoke, his face showed a smile, and the gentle scholar atmosphere was enough to move the younger generation. Among the audience, there was a person with a round face and a slight beard, leaning against the platform, frequently turning his head, as a powerful expression of being convinced. It is also enough to see the depth of Mr. 's speech.

▲ How does Mr. Wang read Wang spoke about how to read books. First, he described three motivations for reading: being forced, for application, and being interested. He also said that the success of reading with interest is the greatest. Secondly, he described the joy of reading, saying that reading is actually chatting with the author. Not only can university scholars far away in Europe and the United States be in the same room, but also ancient sages thousands of years ago can be seen at the desk. The joy is endless. He also said that there are two difficulties in reading: one is the problem of time, and the other is the problem of money. However, both are not difficult to solve. We work eight hours a day and sleep eight hours, and there are still eight hours left, which can be used for reading. If it is halved, there are still four hours a day that can be used for reading. Regarding the issue of money, it is difficult for many people to live at a high level now, and even food and clothing are sometimes in short supply. In fact, we should know that reading should be as important as food and clothing. The stomach must be fed, and the brain must be fed. Hunger in the stomach makes it impossible to work, and an empty brain also makes it impossible to work. Therefore, we should economize on food and clothing to buy books to read. Saving three yuan a month is enough to buy about three hundred-page books. The number of words should be more than 480,000, and 6 million words can be read in a year. Then he described the four essentials of reading: reading more, doing more, seeing more, and thinking more. He also elaborated on the thinking aspect in detail. The main idea is that thinking is not afraid of having fantasies. It is because of fantasies that correct ideas can emerge. However, to have correct ideas, you must understand mathematics and geometry. The Chinese people's so-so, probably, and almost are clear evidence of the lack of mathematical minds. In the future, we must overthrow the so-so, probably, and almost before we can talk about academics. Finally, he said that reading must first identify the goal, what kind of specialized subject you want to learn, and then search for books related to this subject and study them according to a certain procedure, and never be aimless, but only seek to be broad. As a result, those who seek to be broad will not be able to do it, and will become neither fish nor fowl. When Mr. spoke, witty remarks were made frequently, and applause was constant.

Review of "The Jazz Singer" After a Test Screening

— Jin Kaixu

A man named Anderson, who is also a prominent figure in the stage life, recently said that with the advent of sound films, the stage's career will gradually diminish. This is not only the case for stages in small cities, but even the stages in New York will be affected. Since silent films became popular, the society has gained another medium of entertainment for the common people, and drama has already suffered a fatal blow. However, the songs and dances on the stage can be seen but not heard, and the interest is only half as good. Therefore, the stage can never be completely replaced. But now, with the advent of sound films, the mute can speak, the silent can make a sound, and the quiet becomes lively, achieving the wonderful effect of both sound and appearance. Thus, people do not need to watch real-life performances on the stage, but only need to place themselves in front of the silver screen. Every song and dance, every sound and color, can be intoxicating. Moreover, the greatness of sound films is far beyond the reach of the stage. The stage is limited by its location and cannot build a stage comparable to a photography studio. It is also limited by capital and cannot gather dozens or hundreds of stars in one place, or hundreds or thousands of actors in one location. Only films can do this. Understanding this, we can know that the reason why Ziegfeld and Paul Whiteman, who are famous for their songs and dances in New York, must rely on sound films is to fully display their skills. Paul Whiteman is a prominent figure in song and dance, and people even respect him as a king. That is why he is named "The Jazz Singer." "The Jazz Singer" was test-screened at the Nanjing Grand Theater a few days ago. The reporter was invited to watch it and felt its greatness. Not only could it not be performed on the stage, but it was also difficult to compete with among many song and dance films. The whole film is in full color, and the magnificence can be said to have reached the extreme. The abundance of songs and dances is especially evident in the final "Melting Pot of Music," which almost melts the essence of music into one furnace and becomes a modern golden refinement for enjoyment. The famous songs, such as "It Happened in Monterey," "Song of the Dawn," and "I Like to do Things for You," are all structures that were popular for a time.

Rare and Interesting News from the Art World

▲ Yang Du's Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition: The mundane world is unbearably vulgar. On Sunday, I finally had a day of leisure and wanted to find a place to cleanse my ears and eyes, but I couldn't find one. Unexpectedly, I found it in the Nanjing Road in the heart of Xihua, which was truly beyond my expectations. What place is it? It is the Yicheng Calligraphy and Painting Society. The society is hosted by Mr. Qian Huafu. Recently, it is holding the Yang Du Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition. I went there with Mr. Jin Shouchun. We climbed the stairs from Yunnan Road. At that time, it was the time when layman Wan Shaoshi was lecturing on the scriptures. More than twenty people sat solemnly and listened quietly. The topic was the essence of Zen Esoteric Buddhism. Unfortunately, I didn't understand Zen principles, so I looked up at Mr. Yang's calligraphy and paintings. Most of them were vertical scrolls, with iron-like strokes and silver hooks, ancient and unparalleled. His paintings, in particular, had a unique style, beyond Qingxiang Bada. Without natural talent, it would be difficult to create such a wonderful realm. The inscription on the "Cherishing Yin Picture" painted by Huafu, "A moment, thousands of eons," is especially thought-provoking. I sighed in admiration. (Dao Cun)

▲ Yu Yushuang's Posthumous Works Exhibition: Mr. Yu Yushuang, a famous painter from Guian, has become more famous since he passed away. Those who obtain even a small piece of his silk or paper regard it as a treasure. On the fifteenth day of the ninth month of the lunar calendar, it was Yu Yushuang's birthday in the afterlife. Friends Shang Shengbo, Chen Wenfu, Ma Qizhou, Xiong Songquan, Qian Shoutie, Ren Jinshu, Lü Shiqian, Sun Xueni, and Tang Jisheng, etc., set up an altar at Chongfa Temple on Guling Road to offer prayers for his soul. They also held a posthumous works exhibition. Dozens of Mr. Yu's famous paintings were hung on the four walls, including flowers, figures, ladies, and landscapes, all of which were excellent. On both sides of the altar, couplets written by He Tianjian were hung, with extremely detached and powerful words. The couplet written by Qian Shoutie said: "Why bother to write a grand summons? Look at the paintings filling the room, as if the spirit banner is carrying rain. Just to commemorate the birthday, grieving for a hundred years of friendship, the cold flute of the neighborhood presses close, causing people to sigh and admire." In the evening, painters gathered. The host monk prepared a vegetarian meal to entertain the guests and asked for paintings and calligraphy. Shoutie and Tianjian each painted a Luohan, Songquan painted a pair of lions, Qizhou wrote a pair of cranes, Shengbo painted flowers, and Xueni painted landscapes. Jinshu inscribed poems on each of them. A total of eight collaborative works were created. The host monk was overjoyed and bowed with his palms together in worship. By the time the guests dispersed, it was already past midnight. (Yan Zi)

▲ Xing Hua Lou's Pre-exhibition of Ji Chong: I have been writing in Shanghai for three years. Stepping into the art world, I have humbly followed in the footsteps of others. Holding a pen and writing, the ingrained habits are hard to change. Unfortunately, my talent is limited and I am not capable of traveling a thousand miles. However, by persevering and accumulating little by little, I have gradually made progress. Not daring to be complacent with my meager achievements, I held a personal exhibition to seek correction from those who are knowledgeable. Before the exhibition, I held a pre-exhibition at Xing Hua Lou, and I was honored by the gracious presence of many friends and seniors, who gave me advice and encouragement. I was also fortunate to have them order my works in advance, so that all the exhibits were sold out. I am deeply grateful for their kindness and friendship. Mr. Binhong inscribed "True Strength Fills, Energy Flows Like a Rainbow, Encompassing All Things, Obtaining the World." Layman Daqian inscribed "Primordial Energy Drips, the Hanging Still Wet." Mr. Shanzi and Mr. Ying Peng both inscribed "A Dazzling Array." Mr. Yamada Kenkichi inscribed "Artistic Essence." Mr. Tao Min inscribed "Ten Thousand Mountains Gather Verdure." Elder Ruosou inscribed "Forming One's Own School." Mr. Shujuan inscribed "A Myriad of Phenomena." Mr. Jianfu inscribed "A Majestic Atmosphere." Mr. Qingshan Nong inscribed "All Aspects Complete." Mr. Zheng Bai inscribed "Ancient and Lush." Mr. Gong Zhen inscribed "Wonderful Ink and Refined Brush." Mr. Zuyi inscribed "I Cannot Paint, But I Like to Read Paintings, Especially Mr. Yu's Paintings." Mr. Yimin inscribed "Ink Interest Abounds." Mr. Ganyuan inscribed "Clouds and Smoke Pass Before the Eyes." Mr. Shoutie inscribed "Spanning Ancient and Modern." Layman Hongli inscribed "Ethereal and Mysterious." Mr. Manqing inscribed "A Hill and a Ravine Startle People." Mr. Wuchang inscribed "Wandering with the Creator." The praise is excessive, and I cannot help but blush. I should write it on my belt and inscribe it on my seat as a means of encouragement. The exhibition will be held for three days, on the fifteenth, sixteenth, and seventeenth, at the Ningbo Fellow Association on the fourth floor of Xizang Road. I sincerely hope that enlightened people from all walks of life will come to teach me. (Yu Jianhua)

Travel Notes from Nanyang (72)

— Linghua

I asked the host if there were tigers in this place. The host put down his opium pipe and looked displeased. "Don't say that," he said. "You shouldn't say that when you are going out." I asked, "Why not?" He replied, "You can only say 'big object'." I've been here for over ten years and I've never heard anyone say that." I knew that he held a mystical meaning. He also said, "There are also 'small objects', which are leopards." I asked if there were snakes. He said, "You can also call them 'old brushes'. Don't say 'snakes'." I asked if they were harmful. He answered no. However, the host's tone was mystical, so I didn't inquire further.

What I don't understand is the beard of the Indian people. It is extremely long and dirty. They don't know to shave it off. They say that they have kept it since they were young, believing that it is a male attribute used to strengthen their power. I often say that women consider beauty as beauty, while men consider the ability to kill as beauty. That is, they consider great ugliness as beauty. Looking at the beard of the Indian people, it seems to be this meaning.

The Burmese people have a view of life that is both impermanent and pleasure-seeking. This can be proven by their love of theater. The Burmese have the custom of going to the theater from night until dawn. Men and women who love theater sleep together in the theater, indulging in the joys of entertainment. Once, there was an incident in which monks requested to listen to the opera and were stabbed to death by government police. This was caused by the famous Burmese actress Pu Xin. Posing Pu Xin Dan is old now. She is the Mei Lanfang of Burma. Her performance tickets cost four or five shields per person. Now she has hundreds of thousands of dollars. The British government sent two guards to protect her. Pu Xin opposed monks watching the opera and demanded that tickets not be sold to monks. In the middle of the Burmese theater, there are preferential seats for monks. I observed that there were two rows reserved for them, and the tickets were half price. It was like our military. The monks could not oppose Pu Xin, so they confronted the police who were protecting Pu Xin. They even formed a team and fought the police in a bloody battle. As a result, an order was issued prohibiting monks from traveling in groups of two. Two monks had to be fifty steps apart. This lasted for several days. From this, we can see the Burmese people's love of theater and the monks' recklessness.

Warmth in the Heart (315)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Fifteen: Tears Fall in All Directions, Red Emotions in Sadness; A Hall is Captivated, Green Intentions Linger

Among Ling Zhixiang's five or six wives, there are not only Chinese wives but also foreign wives. Two friends who were shocked by the development of women's rights in Europe wondered how difficult the foreign wives were to serve. They asked him how he integrated the East and West into one, not only with a well-managed domestic affairs but also as a diplomatic expert. According to him, foreign wives are also easy to serve. Foreign women have the temperaments of foreign women. If you can grasp their temperaments, there is nothing to fear. They also value face. If you give them face, it will be fine. They also value love. Once they follow you, they prioritize love. Of course, everything can be discussed. Unlike Chinese women, they can be very stubborn and have a special kind of temperament. Neither hard tactics nor soft tactics work. That is really difficult. Foreign women, especially those married from foreign countries, are even more so. When they come to China, they are completely clueless about everything. Even women who grow up in Shanghai mostly associate with foreigners. They don't understand much about the situation in China. They haven't picked up any of the bad habits or bad tempers of Chinese women. As for the bad habits and bad tempers of foreign women, once they marry a Chinese man, Chinese etiquette can be used to restrain them. Therefore, marrying a foreign woman is not difficult to deal with, as long as you handle it properly. However, it is best for foreign wives to live in foreign-style homes and not live with Chinese wives. If a foreign wife lives in the interior and assimilates with Chinese wives, it will be much more difficult. She will learn all the bad habits and bad tempers of Chinese women, plus the inherent bad habits and bad tempers of foreign women, and it will never be good. Many people admire Ling Zhixiang's words. However, there are still few people in China who marry foreign wives. Ling Zhixiang can be considered to have a unique perspective. If another person marries a foreign wife, I wonder what other methods they would use. In short, Ling Zhixiang takes an isolationist approach, so his invitations are also distinguished by order of priority. He doesn't let them meet. As for the invitation card, a large character is added under the character "Ling," which also has a special meaning. Because there are two guests with the surname Ling. One of them, who is also named Ling, seems to be a bit of a rogue. They don't want to invite him, but they are afraid that Ling Zhixiang invited him. It would be bad not to go. So they asked Ling Zhixiang to write a large character under the character "Ling." He is obviously the "Big Ling." The one without the large character is of course the "Little Ling." This is a mark on the invitation card to distinguish between the two. You can then decide whether to go or not. Lin Fanzi wrote down the invitation cards for each person. When he got to Long Ziyun, he said, "You are inviting Bao Meiyun. Let me write it down for you." Long Ziyun said, "No, I'll write 'Green Intentions'."

Sudden Turmoil in the Financial and Gold Markets

▲ Hamaguchi Assassination Disrupts Market: Yesterday, the gold market continued its downward trend, with violent fluctuations that were difficult to predict. The day saw a total of more than seven taels of twists and turns, with sudden drops and jumps, creating extreme confusion. The momentum was unstoppable. Transactions among peers were divided, with some selling first and then buying later. Yuan Maoyong, Taixing, Bingxing, and Taihengyuan, among others, bought in, while Fuchang, Yuanheng, Yu Da, Zhifengyong, and the Dalian gang sold out. The market initially opened low due to rising silver prices overseas. Later, foreign exchange rates also rose by almost half a point, and the domestic market seemed weak. Bank withdrawals were uneven. The gold price was suppressed to eighty-six or eighty-seven taels when news broke of the assassination of Japanese Prime Minister Hamaguchi. As the news spread, the market lost confidence. Major players tended to sell, causing a sudden turmoil and a sharp drop of four or five taels. The situation then eased slightly, but a second telegram reporting the severe nature of his injuries caused another sharp drop of four taels, almost like a river flowing downhill. The price plummeted to slightly above eighty-one taels. Later, the Dalian gang and others resumed buying, while retail investors sold, likely because the swap period had arrived and it was not advisable to sell. In particular, various firms were even mutually swapping in advance, with the bullish side advancing, initially at four or five taels, and later soaring to around seven taels. As a result, the market price rebounded sharply, quickly reaching above eighty-seven taels. However, the situation was vague. Amidst the swap orders, a sudden and unexpected change occurred.

Flour Market Falls Sharply and Recovers Slightly

Yesterday, after the flour market opened, the prices of each month fell one after another. In this month, due to the arrival of foreign wheat from small and medium-sized factories, buyers were afraid that there would be a huge amount of sales and dumping, so they rushed to sell as soon as the market opened, and the market immediately saw a tragic fall. The prices of distant months also mostly followed suit, but there was only a change of 1 fen. This month, however, fell madly by more than 2 fen. In the afternoon, some shorts entered the market, and this month recovered by a few fen. Distant months also followed suit by a few li. At the close, this month was still down by 1 fen and 25 li, December was down by 5 li, January was down by 2.5 li, and February was down by 2.5 li. March and April each fell by 2.5 li.

Wheat Market Tired and Lifeless

Yesterday, after the wheat market opened, both the upper and lower markets were sluggish and unbearable. In fact, after the arrival of two ships of foreign wheat the day before, the market sentiment had already been shaken, and some factories were eager to sell, so there was no hope of a turnaround in the market. At the close in the afternoon, this month was down by 3 fen, next month was down by 1 fen, January was down by 2 fen, February was down by 1 fen, March was unchanged, and April was down by 1 fen. The intake of goods from various factories on the spot was sluggish, and the Tongshi market only recovered 300 bags of wheat at a price of 4 taels and 1 qian and 5 fen, which was also 5 fen weaker than the previous market.

Silk, Tea, and Foreign Firms, Silk Sales Are Lonely and Lifeless

Since the major changes in the French financial sector, the silk market of foreign firms in Shanghai has stagnated, and actual sales have suddenly stopped. Although American firms have intakes of white factories, the overseas prices are surprisingly small, and the difference between the firm and the silk is more than 200 taels, making it difficult to sell. The telegrams of Sichuan dried second warp are also rare, and the market is lonely and lifeless. Yesterday, only Samsung entered 20 bales of HK brand head 234 Mianyang yellow coarse silk at a price of 415 taels.

Silk Factory Cocoon Price is Falling

Since the Shanghai silk factories all suspended business, the Shanghai silk factory cocoon market has suddenly risen sharply. Production has stopped, and the owners are hoarding goods. The market price has risen by 34 taels. The market price of high-quality goods has opened at 26 taels, and the sellers are still unwilling to sell easily. Recently, as the silk factories have resumed work one after another, customers are watching, and the silk factory cocoon market has gradually become weak. The market price of high-quality goods yesterday only opened at 24 taels, and no one has purchased it. The market price is still trending downward.

Gongxi Green Tea's Russian Sales Turn Smooth

Yesterday, the Russian firms of Gongxi green tea from Wuyuan, Tunxi and other places were assisting the association and the intake was getting stronger, and the total turnover of the city was more than 2,000 boxes, and the selling price was unchanged from the previous one. It was found that the current inventory of Gongxi is only more than 10,000 boxes, and the teas from Japan and India have all increased costs due to the high price of gold, and it is impossible to sell to Russia. Therefore, the sales of Gongxi green tea and Qining black tea, which are sold to Russian firms, are still unlimited in the future. Unfortunately, the market is manipulated by its sole proprietor, and tea merchants are still inevitably losing money.
